 sarkari karmchaaree apni kursi par samay se baithne lage or bina kisi aadchan ke apane kaam ko puraa karne lage

 isi tarah immergency se pehle jahaan desh ke vishvavidhyalayon main chaatr raajnneeti charam par thi or or chaatr sanghathan vishvavidhyalayon ko thap kar baithe the, immergency lagu hone ke baad vishvavidhyalayon main padhai shuru ho gai, adhyaaapak samay se apni kakshaon main pahunchane lage or sabase ahm baat yah ki chaatro kii atendence zyaadaatar kakshaon main abhootpurna tareeke se sudharne lagi
 Trains started running on time

 isi tarj par desh main immergency ke dauraan kalabazari par bada waar kiya gaya
 Black marketing, hoarding, illegal trading and broker activities were blocked
 in kaamon main lipt paae jane vaale logon ko bade str par jail main bhar diya gaya

 in phaaydon ke bich aam aadmi par bhi bada asar padaa

 dilli main congress party in dinon bure daur se guzar rahi he
